get\+Offset\+String (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{string}]{\$separator}{ = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\+:\textquotesingle{}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the offset hour and minute formatted with +/-\/ and a given separator ("{}\+:"{} by default). For example, if the time zone is 9 hours 30 minutes, you\textquotesingle{}ll get "{}+09\+:30"{}, with "{}@@"{} as first argument, "{}+09@@30"{}, with "{}"{} as first argument, "{}+0930"{}. Negative offset will return something like "{}-\/12\+:00"{}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
string & {\em \$separator} & string to place between hours and minutes ("{}\+:"{} by default) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Returns raw translation message for a given key.

\hline

\hline

\hline
Translator\+Interface & {\em \$translator} & an optional translator to use\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string 
\end{DoxyReturn}

nth\+Of\+Month (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$nth}{, }\item[{}]{\$day\+Of\+Week}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Modify to the given occurrence of a given day of the week in the current month. If the calculated occurrence is outside the scope of the current month, then return false and no modifications are made. Use the supplied constants to indicate the desired day\+Of\+Week, ex. static\+::\+MONDAY.
